THE DEATH STAR AND STARKVILLE BASE USE TWO DIFFERENT AND ALMOST UNRELATED TECHNOLOGIES

THE DEATH STAR USED GIANT GYBER CRYSTALS LIGHTSABER CRYSTALS TO GENERATE EACH INDIVIDUAL BEAM THIS TYPE OF WEAPON ALLOWED MULTIPLE SMALLER BEANS TO BE CHANGED INTO A SINGLE LARGER BEAM DUE TO THE UNIQUE PROPERTIES OF LIGHTSABERS AT THE COST OF MASSIVE POWER CONSUMPTION

STARKVILLE BASE HOWEVER UTILIZED THE POWER AND MASS OF STARS TO FIRE A SINGLE BEAM OF SUPERHEATED PLASMA AT INCREDIBLE SPEEDS THIS BEAM WAS PRODUCED MUCH IN THE SAME WAY THAT BLASTERS USED TIANA GAS TO CREATE THEIR BOLTS

IF YOU WANT TO KNOW MORE ABOUT LARKIN THEN READ THE BOOK ABOUT HIM LARKIN I AM IT NOW AND THERE IS SOME RELEVANCE TO THE STORY OF THE DEATH STAR IT DOESN'T CONNECT TO ANY OF THE MAIN CHARACTERS OF ROGUE ONE AS IT IS MOSTLY ABOUT RELATIONSHIP TO VADER AND THE EMPEROR AND ALSO HIS ORIGIN STORY HOWEVER IT DOES ALSO GO INTO MOTIVATIONS ABOUT THE DEATH STAR PROJECT BUT JUST A LITTLE BIT AND IN THAT WAY IT HAS SOME RELEVANCE TO HIS RELATIONSHIP TO CRENIC IN BOTH CATALYST AND IN ROGUE ONE IT IS MAINLY JUST BEHIND THE SCENES TYPE OF STORY

IIE Q ROGUE ONE BOOKS
DARTH VADER AFTER MUSTAFAR HAD A SEVERELY REDUCED POTENTIAL BUT HE DID GROW SIGNIFICANTLY STRONGER DESPITE THAT HE WAS AROUND OF POWER BY THE TIME HE DIED

AS FOR CLONE WARS ANAKIN VS LUKE OR DARTH PLAGUERS WE DON'T HAVE A CLEAR PICTURE OF JUST HOW POWERFUL LUKE AND PLAGUERS ARE BUT ANAKIN WAS ONE OF THE MOST POWERFUL JEDI OF HIS ERA

AS FAR AS WE KNOW PALATINE WAS THE MOST POWERFUL FORCE USER OF HIS TIME WITH PERHAPS THE EXCEPTION OF THE ONES ON MORTIS
CANONICALLY SPEAKING ANAKIN WAS RECKONED TO BE TWICE AS POWERFUL AS PALATINE AFTER HIS INJURIES AND TRANSFORMATION IT WAS SAID HE WAS THEN SEVERELY DIMINISHED IN HIS FORCE POWERS ONLY AS POWERFUL AS PALATINE HARD TO KNOW ABOUT LUKE HE WAS STILL VERY MUCH COMING INTO HIS POWER DURING RETURN OF THE JEDI AND WE'VE YET TO SEE WHERE HE WENT FROM THERE BASED ON WHAT WE KNOW I WOULD SAY ANAKIN WAS TRULY FAFFY THE MOST POWERFUL FORCE BEING BUT LACKED THE MATURITY AND GENERAL TEMPERAMENT TO MAKE THE MOST OF HIS POWER
ALOT OF PEOPLE ARE THROWING OUT THE POWER OF PALATINE THING THAT HAS BEEN LATCHED ONTO OVER THE YEARS THIS WAS A STATEMENT MADE BY GEORGE LUCAS YEARS AGO WHETHER THIS IS LITERAL AND ACCURATE OR UP TO DATE IS HIGHLY DEBATABLE LUCAS HAS SAID SO MANY THINGS OUTSIDE OF CANON THAT HAS CHANGED OVER THE YEARS AND NEW CANON SHOWS VADER TO BE A DIFFERENT BEAST
VADER GREW MUCH MORE POWERFUL THAN ANAKIN EVER WAS AND BY WHAT WE'RE SEEING IN NEW CANON AND HOW HE STACKS AGAINST THE EMPEROR HE MAY BE EVEN MORE THAN AS POWERFUL AS PALATINE WHATEVER EDGE PALATINE HAS IN FORCE MASTERY AND POWER VADER DOES MAKE UP FOR IN PHYSICALITY AND COMBAT ABILITY

THAT'S HOW IT WAS IN LEGENDS BUT THAT ISN'T HOW IT IS IN CANON IN CANON FORCE GHOSTS ARE PEOPLE WHO HAVE LEARNED TO PRESERVE THEIR CONSCIOUSNESS IN THE FORCE

NORMALLY WHEN A PERSON DIES THEIR CONSCIOUSNESS AND SELF BECOME ONE WITH THE FORCE THEY FEED FROM THE LIVING FORCE BACK INTO THE GREATER COSMIC FORCE

HOWEVER WITH THE RIGHT TRAINING A PERSON CAN LEARN TO PRESERVE THEIR CONSCIOUSNESS AFTER THEY DIE PREVENTING IT FROM BEING LOST WITHIN THE COSMIC FORCE THEY ESSENTIALLY CAN SEPARATE THEIR CONSCIOUSNESS FROM THE COSMIC FORCE IN THE FORM OF A SPIRIT
